### 1. GET /api/v1/cpgs
**Description:** Client HTTP query request
**Confidence Score:** 0.90

**Entities:**
- {'name': 'total', 'datatype': 'number (int32)', 'description': 'Returns the total number of objects in the collection.'}
- {'name': 'members', 'datatype': 'Array of objects', 'description': 'CPG properties. Returns a JSON array of zero or more JSON objects.'}
- {'name': 'domain', 'datatype': 'string (name31)', 'description': 'Domain to which the CPG belongs.'}
- {'name': 'id', 'datatype': 'number (uint32)', 'description': 'CPG ID.'}
- {'name': 'name', 'datatype': 'string (name31)', 'description': 'CPG name.'}
- {'name': 'numFPVVs', 'datatype': 'number (uint32)', 'description': 'Number of FPVVs allocated in the CPG.'}
- {'name': 'numTDVVs', 'datatype': 'number (uint32)', 'description': 'Number of TDVVs created in the CPG. (WSAPI 1.4.1 and later.)'}
- {'name': 'numTPVVs', 'datatype': 'number (uint32)', 'description': 'Number of TPVVs allocated in the CPG.'}
- {'name': 'SAUsage', 'datatype': 'object', 'description': 'Snapshot administration usage.', 'properties': [{'name': 'totalMiB', 'datatype': 'number (uint64)', 'description': 'Total space usage in MiB.'}, {'name': 'usedMiB', 'datatype': 'number (uint64)', 'description': 'Used space in MiB.'}, {'name': 'freeMiB', 'datatype': 'number (uint64)', 'description': 'Free space in MiB.'}, {'name': 'percentUsed', 'datatype': 'number (uint32)', 'description': 'Percentage of space used.'}]}
- {'name': 'SDUsage', 'datatype': 'object', 'description': 'Snapshot data space usage.', 'properties': [{'name': 'totalMiB', 'datatype': 'number (uint64)', 'description': 'Total space usage in MiB.'}, {'name': 'usedMiB', 'datatype': 'number (uint64)', 'description': 'Used space in MiB.'}, {'name': 'freeMiB', 'datatype': 'number (uint64)', 'description': 'Free space in MiB.'}, {'name': 'percentUsed', 'datatype': 'number (uint32)', 'description': 'Percentage of space used.'}]}
- {'name': 'UsrUsage', 'datatype': 'object', 'description': 'User data space usage.', 'properties': [{'name': 'totalMiB', 'datatype': 'number (uint64)', 'description': 'Total space usage in MiB.'}, {'name': 'usedMiB', 'datatype': 'number (uint64)', 'description': 'Used space in MiB.'}, {'name': 'freeMiB', 'datatype': 'number (uint64)', 'description': 'Free space in MiB.'}, {'name': 'percentUsed', 'datatype': 'number (uint32)', 'description': 'Percentage of space used.'}]}
- {'name': 'uuid', 'datatype': 'string (uuid string)', 'description': 'The UUID that was automatically assigned to the CPG at creation.'}
- {'name': 'warningPct', 'datatype': 'number (uint32)', 'description': 'Percentage usage at which to issue an alert.'}
- {'name': 'SAGrowth', 'datatype': 'object', 'description': 'Snapshot administration space auto-growth parameters.', 'properties': [{'name': 'enabled', 'datatype': 'boolean', 'description': 'Indicates if auto-growth is enabled.'}, {'name': 'growthMiB', 'datatype': 'number (uint64)', 'description': 'Amount of space to grow in MiB when triggered.'}, {'name': 'maxMiB', 'datatype': 'number (uint64)', 'description': 'Maximum space allowed for auto-growth in MiB.'}, {'name': 'thresholdPct', 'datatype': 'number (uint32)', 'description': 'Threshold percentage to trigger auto-growth.'}]}
- {'name': 'SDGrowth', 'datatype': 'object', 'description': 'Snapshot data space auto-growth parameters.', 'properties': [{'name': 'enabled', 'datatype': 'boolean', 'description': 'Indicates if auto-growth is enabled.'}, {'name': 'growthMiB', 'datatype': 'number (uint64)', 'description': 'Amount of space to grow in MiB when triggered.'}, {'name': 'maxMiB', 'datatype': 'number (uint64)', 'description': 'Maximum space allowed for auto-growth in MiB.'}, {'name': 'thresholdPct', 'datatype': 'number (uint32)', 'description': 'Threshold percentage to trigger auto-growth.'}]}
- {'name': 'state', 'datatype': 'number', 'description': 'Overall state of the CPG.', 'enumeration': [{'value': 0, 'meaning': 'Unknown state'}, {'value': 1, 'meaning': 'OK'}, {'value': 2, 'meaning': 'Warning'}, {'value': 3, 'meaning': 'Error'}]}
